INNER JOIN "Categories" AS c ON e."CategoryId" = c."CategoryId"
LEFT JOIN "Purchases" AS p ON e."EventId" = p."EventId"
ORDER BY e."EventId", c."CategoryId"

    SELECT e."EventId", e."Address", e."AvailableTickets", e."CategoryId", e."Description", e."ImagePath", e."OrganizerId", e."Price", e."StartAt", e."Title", c."CategoryId" AS "CategoryId0", c."Description" AS "Description0", c."Name"
